---
about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> This lecture covers the
  lateral geniculate nucleus and the visual cortex, including V1, extrastriate cortex,
  V2, V4, MT, MST and inferotemporal cortex areas.</p><p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Peter H Schiller</p>
